\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01576}01576\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ regressors\ on\ various\ sub-\/samples\ of\ the\ dataset\ and\ uses\ averaging\ to}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01578}01578\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Trees\ in\ the\ forest\ use\ the\ best\ split\ strategy,\ i.e.\ equivalent\ to\ passing}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01583}01583\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01584}01584\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ This\ estimator\ has\ native\ support\ for\ missing\ values\ (NaNs).\ During\ training,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01585}01585\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ the\ tree\ grower\ learns\ at\ each\ split\ point\ whether\ samples\ with\ missing\ values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01586}01586\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ should\ go\ to\ the\ left\ or\ right\ child,\ based\ on\ the\ potential\ gain.\ When\ predicting,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01587}01587\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ samples\ with\ missing\ values\ are\ assigned\ to\ the\ left\ or\ right\ child\ consequently.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01588}01588\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ If\ no\ missing\ values\ were\ encountered\ for\ a\ given\ feature\ during\ training,\ then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01589}01589\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ samples\ with\ missing\ values\ are\ mapped\ to\ whichever\ child\ has\ the\ most\ samples.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l01953}01953\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ to\ split\ the\ non-\/missing\ values\ on.\ Then\ the\ non-\/missing\ values\ will\ be\ sent}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l02331}02331\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ randomized\ decision\ trees\ (a.k.a.\ extra-\/trees)\ on\ various\ sub-\/samples}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l02334}02334\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l02335}02335\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ This\ estimator\ has\ native\ support\ for\ missing\ values\ (NaNs)\ for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l02336}02336\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ random\ splits.\ During\ training,\ a\ random\ threshold\ will\ be\ chosen}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l02337}02337\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ to\ split\ the\ non-\/missing\ values\ on.\ Then\ the\ non-\/missing\ values\ will\ be\ sent}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l02338}02338\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ to\ the\ left\ and\ right\ child\ based\ on\ the\ randomly\ selected\ threshold,\ while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l02339}02339\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ the\ missing\ values\ will\ also\ be\ randomly\ sent\ to\ the\ left\ or\ right\ child.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l02340}02340\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ This\ is\ repeated\ for\ every\ feature\ considered\ at\ each\ split.\ The\ best\ split}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__forest_8py_source_l02341}02341\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ among\ these\ is\ chosen.}}
